<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> (1251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">billet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bilét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ticket (admission to entertainment or transportation)</li>
<li>banknote</li>
<li>membership card</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The noun <b><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></b> in a sense of a ticket can be further described with <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>. For example on entertainment:
</p>
<dl><dd><ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опера.html>о́перу</a> (<i>opera ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цирк.html>цирк</a> (<i>circus ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:балет.html>бале́т</a> (<i>ballet ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>вечер</a> (<i>soiree ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:концерт.html>конце́рт</a> (<i>concert ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:матч.html>матч</a> (<i>sport's match ticket</i>)
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:футбол.html>футбо́л</a> (<i>soccer ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоккей.html>хокке́й</a> (<i>hockey ticket</i>)</li></ul></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тр</a> (<i>theater ticket</i>)</li></ul></dd></dl>
<p>For example on transportation:
</p>
<dl><dd><ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бус</a> (<i>bus ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> самолёт (<i>airplane ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>поезд</a> (<i>train ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скоростной.html>скоростно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>поезд</a> (<i>high-speed train ticket</i>)</li></ul></dd></dl>

<ol><li>биллиард (устар. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a>), шарокат (<a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>прост</a>.)</li>

***бинтовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бинтовать.html>бинтова́ть</a> (29001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бинт.html>бинт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bint</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бинтовать.html>бинтова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bintovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забинтовать.html>забинтова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bandage</li></ol>

***биографический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:биографический.html>биографи́ческий</a> (22930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биография.html>биогра́фия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">biográfija</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">biography</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***бирка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рка</a> (25625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. There are several hypotheses: a borrowing from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:North Germanic languages">North Germanic</a></span> word for birch, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">birk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">bjerk</i>; a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">bir + iki</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one + two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; or a derivation from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">събьрати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭbĭrati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to assemble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bьrati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bírka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nameplate, label, tag</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tally stick <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">notched piece of wood used for keeping an account</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***бирюзовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a> (12546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бирюза́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">birjuzá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">birjuzóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> turquoise <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stone or color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">turquoise colour: <span style="background-color:48D1CC; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>birjuzóvyj</b> cvet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">turquoise <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>turquoise</b> color</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a></b> зиморо́док</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>birjuzóvyj</b> zimoródok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shining-blue_kingfisher" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:shining-blue kingfisher">shining-blue kingfisher</a></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>turquoise</b> kingfisher</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бисер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сер</a> (20745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">бисьръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bisĭrŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pearls</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgar language">Bulgar</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بُسْر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">busr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unripe dates</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from the root <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">ب س ر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">b-s-r</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> related to things being early, so applied to pearls because unripe dates can have some tactile and optical properties similar to pearls.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bíser</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сера</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>beads
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышивать.html>вышива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyšivátʹ bíserom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bead</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышивка.html>вы́шивка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výšivka bíserom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beading, beadwork</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>сви́ньями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">metátʹ bíser péred svínʹjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cast pearls before swine</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бистро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бистро.html>бистро́</a> (30090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bistro</i>, according to folk etymology version borrowed from Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">býstro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> "quickly" in 1814, when Russian Army was in Paris.
</p><p>In actual fact, the word is pure French, first attested only in 1884, possibly from <i>bistingot</i> (pub).
Especially the last letter 't' completely excludes Russian origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бистро.html>бистро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bistró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>bistro</li></ol>

</td></tr></tbody></table><br>Существительное<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение_2">Значение</span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:музыкальный.html>музыка́льное</a>">муз.</span> элементарная единица музыкального метра <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Любая музыка разбита на фразы. Их можно распознать слушая исполнение песни (обычно между фразами певцы вдыхают в грудь воздух). Фразы разбиты на такты, которые в свою очередь, делятся на <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">биты</span>, или доли (им соответствуют щелчки метронома). </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Жёсткость и однообразие <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">бита</span> позволили остальным музыкантам играть чуть-чуть не в такт, иначе говоря, то торопиться, то опаздывать относительно основного <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">бита</span>: это офф-бит (off-beat). </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:музыкальный.html>музыка́льное</a>">муз.</span> музыкальное течение, зародившийся в Великобритании в начале 60-х годов XX века <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Кроме того, широко представлен всякий недурной лаунж (Beanfield, Jazzanova, Shantel, особенно Boozoo Bajou), много типичного тевтонского <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">бита</span> (техно, хаус и пр). </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:театральный.html>театра́льное</a>">театр.</span> небольшой промежуток времени между репликами или действиями <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:битва.html>би́тва</a> (4135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*<a href = vnd.unilang:битва.html>би́тва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*bitva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bitva</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*biti</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tva</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
